--------------------
File: /music-downloader/deploy.sh
--------------------

#!/bin/bash

# Music Downloader Deployment Script
# Usage: ./deploy.sh [build|deploy|clean]

set -e

PROJECT_NAME="music-downloader"
IMAGE_NAME="music-downloader-app"
CONTAINER_NAME="music-downloader-container"

echo "ğŸµ Music Downloader Deployment Script"
echo "====================================="

case "$1" in
    
    deploy)
        echo "ğŸš€ Deploying application with Docker Compose..."
        
        # Stop existing services
        echo "Stopping existing services..."
        docker-compose -f /home/docker-app/music-downloader/docker-compose.yml down 2>/dev/null || true
        
        # Start services with build
        echo "Building and starting services..."
        docker-compose -f /home/docker-app/music-downloader/docker-compose.yml up -d --build
        
        echo "âœ… Deployment completed!"
        echo "Application is running on http://localhost"
        ;;
    
    clean)
        echo "ğŸ§¹ Cleaning up Docker Compose services..."
        docker-compose -f /home/docker-app/music-downloader/docker-compose.yml down -v 2>/dev/null || true
        docker-compose -f /home/docker-app/music-downloader/docker-compose.yml rm -f 2>/dev/null || true
        echo "âœ… Cleanup completed!"
        ;;
    
    *)
        echo "Usage: $0 [build|deploy|clean]"
        echo ""
        echo "Commands:"
        echo "  deploy  - Deploy the application using Docker Compose"
        echo "  clean   - Clean up Docker Compose services"
        echo ""
        echo "Examples:"
        echo "  $0 deploy"
        echo "  $0 clean"
        exit 1
        ;;
esac

--------------------
File: /music-downloader/docker-compose.yml
--------------------

version: '3.8'

services:
  music-downloader:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "80:80"
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
    networks:
      - app-network
    volumes:
      - /home/docker-app/music-downloader/dist:/usr/share/nginx/html
      - /home/docker-app/music-downloader/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf

networks:
  app-network:
    external: true

File: /music-downloader/nginx.conf
--------------------

user  nginx;
worker_processes  auto;

error_log  /var/log/nginx/error.log warn;
pid        /var/run/nginx.pid;

events {
    worker_connections  1024;
}

http {
    include       /etc/nginx/mime.types;
    default_type  application/octet-stream;

    log_format  main  '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                      '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" "$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for"';

    access_log  /var/log/nginx/access.log  main;

    sendfile        on;
    #tcp_nopush     on;

    keepalive_timeout  65;

    #gzip  on;

    server {
        listen       80;
        server_name  localhost;
        
        # é˜²æ­¢ç‚¹å‡»åŠ«æŒæ”»å‡»
        add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN;
        add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;
        add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block";

        # Vue é¡¹ç›®æ ¹ç›®å½•
        root   /usr/share/nginx/html;
        index  index.html index.htm;

        # å¤„ç† Vue Router çš„ History æ¨¡å¼
        location / {
            try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        }

        location ^~/api/ {
            # å…è®¸æ‰€æœ‰åŸŸè·¨åŸŸè®¿é—®ï¼ˆä¸æ¨èï¼Œå‡ºäºå®‰å…¨è€ƒè™‘åº”æŒ‡å®šå…·ä½“åŸŸåï¼‰
            # add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin' '*';

            proxy_pass http://music-downloader-backend-music-downloader-backend-1:3000/;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;

            # å…è®¸ç‰¹å®šåŸŸè·¨åŸŸè®¿é—®ï¼ˆæ¨èï¼‰
            add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin' '*';

            # å…è®¸çš„HTTPæ–¹æ³•
            add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Methods' 'GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, OPTIONS';

            # å…è®¸çš„è‡ªå®šä¹‰è¯·æ±‚å¤´
            add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Headers' 'Content-Type, Authorization, X-Requested-With';

            # å…è®¸æºå¸¦Cookie
            add_header 'Access-Control-Allow-Credentials' 'true';

            # é¢„æ£€è¯·æ±‚çš„æœ‰æ•ˆæœŸï¼ˆå¯é€‰ï¼‰
            add_header 'Access-Control-Max-Age' 1728000;

            # å¦‚æœè¯·æ±‚æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯OPTIONSï¼Œåˆ™ç›´æ¥è¿”å›204çŠ¶æ€ç ï¼Œä¸æ‰§è¡Œåç»­æ“ä½œ
            if ($request_method = 'OPTIONS') {
                return 204;
            }

            # å…¶ä»–é…ç½®...
        }

        # ç¼“å­˜é™æ€èµ„æº
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg)$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, immutable";
        }

        # ç¦æ­¢è®¿é—® .ht æ–‡ä»¶
        location ~ /\.ht {
            deny all;
        }
    }
}

File: /music-downloader/src/utils/filename.js

// src/utils/filename.js
// æ–‡ä»¶å‘½åå·¥å…·å‡½æ•°

/**
 * æ¸…ç†æ–‡ä»¶åä¸­çš„éæ³•å­—ç¬¦
 * @param {string} filename - åŸå§‹æ–‡ä»¶å
 * @returns {string} æ¸…ç†åçš„æ–‡ä»¶å
 */
export const sanitizeFilename = (filename) => {
  if (!filename) return 'unknown';
  
  return filename
    // æ›¿æ¢Windowsä¸å…è®¸çš„å­—ç¬¦
    .replace(/[<>:"/\\|?*]/g, '_')
    // æ›¿æ¢æ§åˆ¶å­—ç¬¦ï¼ˆESLintå¿½ç•¥æ§åˆ¶å­—ç¬¦æ£€æŸ¥ï¼‰
    /* eslint-disable no-control-regex */
    .replace(/[\u0000-\u001F\u007F-\u009F]/g, '_')
    /* eslint-enable no-control-regex */
    // åˆå¹¶å¤šä¸ªè¿ç»­çš„ä¸‹åˆ’çº¿
    .replace(/_+/g, '_')
    // åˆå¹¶å¤šä¸ªç©ºæ ¼
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
    // å»é™¤é¦–å°¾ç©ºæ ¼å’Œä¸‹åˆ’çº¿
    .trim()
    .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, '');
};

/**
 * ç”Ÿæˆè§„èŒƒçš„éŸ³ä¹æ–‡ä»¶å
 * æ ¼å¼: æ­Œæ‰‹ - æ­Œæ›²å.æ‰©å±•å
 * @param {Object} song - æ­Œæ›²å¯¹è±¡
 * @param {string} extension - æ–‡ä»¶æ‰©å±•å
 * @returns {string} å®Œæ•´çš„æ–‡ä»¶å
 */
export const generateMusicFilename = (song, extension = 'mp3') => {
  // è·å–æ­Œæ‰‹åå’Œæ­Œæ›²åï¼Œæä¾›é»˜è®¤å€¼
  const singerName = song.SingerName || song.singer || song.artist || 'æœªçŸ¥æ­Œæ‰‹';
  const songName = song.OriSongName || song.songName || song.title || 'æœªçŸ¥æ­Œæ›²';
  
  // æ¸…ç†æ­Œæ‰‹åå’Œæ­Œæ›²å
  const cleanSinger = sanitizeFilename(singerName);
  const cleanSong = sanitizeFilename(songName);
  
  // ç»„åˆæ–‡ä»¶å
  let filename = `${cleanSinger} - ${cleanSong}`;
  
  // æ·»åŠ æ‰©å±•å
  if (extension) {
    filename += `.${extension.toLowerCase()}`;
  }
  
  // é™åˆ¶æ–‡ä»¶åé•¿åº¦ï¼ˆWindowsæœ€å¤§255å­—ç¬¦ï¼‰
  if (filename.length > 200) {
    const ext = extension ? `.${extension.toLowerCase()}` : '';
    const maxLength = 200 - ext.length;
    filename = `${filename.substring(0, maxLength)}${ext}`;
  }
  
  return filename;
};

/**
 * ä»URLè·å–æ–‡ä»¶æ‰©å±•å
 * @param {string} url - æ–‡ä»¶URL
 * @returns {string} æ‰©å±•å
 */
export const getFileExtensionFromUrl = (url) => {
  if (!url) return 'mp3';
  
  try {
    const urlObj = new URL(url);
    const pathname = urlObj.pathname;
    const ext = pathname.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
    
    // å¸¸è§éŸ³é¢‘æ ¼å¼æ˜ å°„
    const audioExtensions = {
      'mp3': 'mp3',
      'flac': 'flac',
      'wav': 'wav',
      'aac': 'aac',
      'm4a': 'm4a',
      'ogg': 'ogg',
      'wma': 'wma'
    };
    
    return audioExtensions[ext] || 'mp3';
  } catch (error) {
    console.warn('è§£æURLæ‰©å±•åå¤±è´¥:', error);
    return 'mp3';
  }
};

/**
 * ç›´æ¥è§¦å‘æ–‡ä»¶ä¸‹è½½
 * @param {string} url - æ–‡ä»¶ä¸‹è½½URL
 * @param {string} filename - æ–‡ä»¶å
 */
export const triggerDownload = (url, filename) => {
  try {
    // åˆ›å»ºéšè—çš„ä¸‹è½½é“¾æ¥
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.download = filename;
    link.style.display = 'none';
    
    // æ·»åŠ åˆ°DOMå¹¶è§¦å‘ç‚¹å‡»
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    
    // å»¶è¿Ÿæ¸…ç†DOMå…ƒç´ 
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (document.body.contains(link)) {
        document.body.removeChild(link);
      }
    }, 1000);
    
    console.log(`å¼€å§‹ä¸‹è½½æ–‡ä»¶: ${filename}`);
    return true;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('è§¦å‘ä¸‹è½½å¤±è´¥:', error);
    return false;
  }
};

--------------------
File: /music-downloader/src/utils/token.js
--------------------

export const setToken = (userData)=>{
    localStorage.setItem('token', userData.token);
    localStorage.setItem('vip_token', userData.vip_token);
    localStorage.setItem('userid', userData.userid);
    localStorage.setItem('vip_type', userData.vip_type);
}

export const removeToken = ()=>{
    localStorage.removeItem('token');
    localStorage.removeItem('vip_token');
    localStorage.removeItem('userid');
    localStorage.removeItem('vip_type');
}

export const getToken = ()=>{
    return {
        token: localStorage.getItem('token'),
        vip_token: localStorage.getItem('vip_token'),
        userid: localStorage.getItem('userid'),
        vip_type: localStorage.getItem('vip_type'),
    }
}

// src/services/api.js
import axios from 'axios';

// åˆ›å»ºaxioså®ä¾‹
const apiClient = axios.create({
  baseURL: import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL,
  timeout: 30000,
  withCredentials: true,
  headers: {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  }
});

// è¯·æ±‚æ‹¦æˆªå™¨
apiClient.interceptors.request.use(
  (config) => {
    // æ·»åŠ è®¤è¯ä¿¡æ¯
    const auth = localStorage.getItem('auth');
    if (auth) {
      const cookie = Object.entries(JSON.parse(auth))
        .map(([k, v]) => `${k}=${v}`)
        .join('; ');
      config.headers.Cookie = cookie;
    }
    console.log('è¯·æ±‚:', config.baseURL + config.url);
    return config;
  },
  (error) => {
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

// å“åº”æ‹¦æˆªå™¨
apiClient.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => {
    console.log('å“åº”:', response);
    return response.data;
  },
  (error) => {
    console.error('è¯·æ±‚é”™è¯¯:', error);
    if (error.response?.status === 502) {
      throw new Error(error.response.data?.error_msg || 'æœåŠ¡å™¨é”™è¯¯');
    }
    throw error;
  }
);

export const request = async (endpoint, options = {}) => {
    // æ„é€ å®Œæ•´ URL
    let url = `${import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL}${endpoint}`;
    console.log('request......', url)
    const auth = localStorage.getItem('auth');
    // å°†storeä¸­çš„cookieè½¬æ¢ä¸ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå¹¶è®¾ç½®åˆ°è¯·æ±‚å¤´ä¸­
    const cookie = auth ? Object.entries(auth).map(([k, v]) => `${k}=${v}`).join('; ') : '';

    const headers = {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Cookie': cookie,
        ...options.headers,
    };

    options = {
        ...options,
        headers,
    }


    return fetch(url, { ...options, credentials: 'include' })
        .then((res) => {
            console.log('res', res)
            if (res.status === 502) {
                return res.json().then((data) => {
                    throw new Error(data.error_msg)
                })
            }
            return res.json()
        })
        .then((data) => {
            console.log('data', data)
            return data
        })
        .catch((error) => {
            throw new Error(error);
        });
}


export const getSongUrl = (hash) => request(`/song/url?hash=${hash}&quality=320`);

// åŸºäºaxiosçš„æ–‡ä»¶ä¸‹è½½åŠŸèƒ½
export const downloadSong = async (hash, filename) => {
  try {
    // è·å–æ­Œæ›²URL
    const songData = await getSongUrl(hash);
    
    if (!songData?.backupUrl?.[0]) {
      throw new Error('æ— æ³•è·å–æ­Œæ›²ä¸‹è½½åœ°å€');
    }
    
    const downloadUrl = songData.backupUrl[0];
    const extension = songData.extName || 'mp3';
    
    // ä½¿ç”¨axiosä¸‹è½½æ–‡ä»¶
    const response = await axios({
      method: 'GET',
      url: downloadUrl,
      responseType: 'blob',
      timeout: 60000, // 60ç§’è¶…æ—¶
      onDownloadProgress: (progressEvent) => {
        // å¯ä»¥åœ¨è¿™é‡Œæ·»åŠ ä¸‹è½½è¿›åº¦å›è°ƒ
        const percentCompleted = Math.round(
          (progressEvent.loaded * 100) / progressEvent.total
        );
        console.log(`ä¸‹è½½è¿›åº¦: ${percentCompleted}%`);
      }
    });
    
    // åˆ›å»ºæ–‡ä»¶å¯¹è±¡
    const blob = new Blob([response.data], {
      type: response.headers['content-type'] || 'audio/mpeg'
    });
    
    // ç”Ÿæˆæœ€ç»ˆæ–‡ä»¶å
    const finalFilename = filename || `æ­Œæ›²_${Date.now()}.${extension}`;
    
    // è§¦å‘ä¸‹è½½
    const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.download = finalFilename;
    link.style.display = 'none';
    
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    
    // æ¸…ç†èµ„æº
    setTimeout(() => {
      document.body.removeChild(link);
      window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    }, 100);
    
    console.log(`ä¸‹è½½å®Œæˆ: ${finalFilename}`);
    return { success: true, filename: finalFilename };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('ä¸‹è½½å¤±è´¥:', error);
    throw new Error(`ä¸‹è½½å¤±è´¥: ${error.message}`);
  }
};

// è·å–ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢å›¾ç‰‡
export const getAlbumImages = (hash, albumId = '') => {
  const params = new URLSearchParams();
  params.append('hash', hash);
  if (albumId) {
    params.append('album_id', albumId);
  }
  // æ ¹æ®å®é™…APIè°ƒæ•´å‚æ•°
  params.append('count', '5'); // è·å–å¤šå¼ å›¾ç‰‡ä»¥ç¡®ä¿èƒ½æ‰¾åˆ°åˆé€‚çš„å°é¢
  
  return request(`/images?${params.toString()}`);
};

// src/pages/Home.jsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from "react";
import { useNavigate, useLocation } from "react-router-dom";
import { Spin, Empty, message    } from "antd";
import {
  PlayCircleOutlined,
  DownloadOutlined,
  UserOutlined,
  DatabaseOutlined,
  LoadingOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons";
import {
  request,
  getSongUrl,
  getAlbumImages,
  downloadSong,
} from "../services/api";
import { generateMusicFilename } from "../utils/filename";
import { usePlayer } from "../contexts/PlayerContext";
import { useSearch } from "../contexts/SearchContext";

const Home = () => {
  const [songs, setSongs] = useState([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [isLazyLoading, setIsLazyLoading] = useState(false);
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const [total, setTotal] = useState(0);
  const [pageSize] = useState(15);
  const [hasMore, setHasMore] = useState(true);
  const [albumImages, setAlbumImages] = useState({}); // å­˜å‚¨ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢å›¾ç‰‡URL
  const observerRef = useRef();

  const { playSong } = usePlayer();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();
  const { searchKeyword, finishSearch } = useSearch();

  // è·å–ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢å›¾ç‰‡
  const fetchAlbumImage = async (song) => {
    try {
      const res = await getAlbumImages(song.FileHash, song.AlbumID || "");
      console.log("ä¸“è¾‘å›¾ç‰‡APIå“åº”:", res);

      if (res.data && res.data.length > 0) {
        // æ ¹æ®å®é™…è¿”å›æ ¼å¼è§£æä¸“è¾‘å°é¢
        let imageUrl = "";

        // ä¼˜å…ˆæ£€æŸ¥ album æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„ sizable_cover
        if (res.data[0].album && res.data[0].album.length > 0) {
          const album = res.data[0].album[0];
          console.log("æ‰¾åˆ°ä¸“è¾‘ä¿¡æ¯:", album);
          imageUrl = album.sizable_cover || "";
          // æ›¿æ¢ {size} ä¸ºå®é™…å°ºå¯¸
          if (imageUrl) {
            imageUrl = imageUrl.replace("{size}", "200");
            console.log("ä½¿ç”¨ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢:", imageUrl);
          }
        }

        // å¦‚æœ album ä¸­æ²¡æœ‰æ‰¾åˆ°ï¼Œæ£€æŸ¥ author ä¸­çš„å›¾ç‰‡
        if (!imageUrl && res.data[0].author && res.data[0].author.length > 0) {
          const author = res.data[0].author[0];
          console.log("ä½¿ç”¨æ­Œæ‰‹ä¿¡æ¯:", author);

          // ä¼˜å…ˆä½¿ç”¨ imgs['3'] ä¸­çš„å›¾ç‰‡
          if (author.imgs && author.imgs["3"] && author.imgs["3"].length > 0) {
            imageUrl = author.imgs["3"][0]?.sizable_portrait || "";
            if (imageUrl) {
              imageUrl = imageUrl.replace("{size}", "200");
              console.log("ä½¿ç”¨æ­Œæ‰‹å›¾ç‰‡[3]:", imageUrl);
            }
          }
          // å…¶æ¬¡ä½¿ç”¨ imgs['4'] ä¸­çš„å›¾ç‰‡
          else if (
            author.imgs &&
            author.imgs["4"] &&
            author.imgs["4"].length > 0
          ) {
            imageUrl = author.imgs["4"][0]?.sizable_portrait || "";
            if (imageUrl) {
              imageUrl = imageUrl.replace("{size}", "200");
              console.log("ä½¿ç”¨æ­Œæ‰‹å›¾ç‰‡[4]:", imageUrl);
            }
          }
          // æœ€åä½¿ç”¨ avatar
          else if (author.sizable_avatar) {
            imageUrl = author.sizable_avatar.replace("{size}", "200");
            console.log("ä½¿ç”¨æ­Œæ‰‹å¤´åƒ:", imageUrl);
          }
        }

        if (imageUrl) {
          console.log(`ä¸ºæ­Œæ›² ${song.OriSongName} è®¾ç½®å°é¢:`, imageUrl);
          setAlbumImages((prev) => ({
            ...prev,
            [song.FileHash]: imageUrl,
          }));
        } else {
          console.log("æœªæ‰¾åˆ°æœ‰æ•ˆçš„å°é¢å›¾ç‰‡");
        }
      } else {
        console.log("APIè¿”å›ç©ºæ•°æ®");
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("è·å–ä¸“è¾‘å›¾ç‰‡å¤±è´¥:", error);
      // å³ä½¿è·å–å¤±è´¥ä¹Ÿä¸å½±å“ä¸»æµç¨‹
    }
  };

  const searchSongs = useCallback(
    async (page = 1) => {
      // å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰å…³é”®è¯ä¸”ä¸æ˜¯åˆ†é¡µæ“ä½œï¼Œæç¤ºç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥
      if (!searchKeyword?.trim() && page === 1) {
        // ä¸å†å¼¹å‡ºalertï¼Œè®©ç”¨æˆ·è‡ªå·±è¾“å…¥
        return;
      }

      // å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰å…³é”®è¯ä½†æœ‰åˆ†é¡µæ“ä½œï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ä¹‹å‰çš„å…³é”®è¯
      const keyword = searchKeyword?.trim() || "";

      if (!keyword) {
        return;
      }

      try {
        setIsLoading(true);
        const res = await request(
          `/search?type=song&keywords=${keyword}&page=${page}&pagesize=${pageSize}`
        );
        const data = res.data;
        if (page === 1) {
          setSongs(data.lists || []);
          // ä¸ºæ–°æœç´¢ç»“æœè·å–ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢
          (data.lists || []).forEach((song) => {
            fetchAlbumImage(song);
          });
        } else {
          const newSongs = data.lists || [];
          setSongs((prevSongs) => [...prevSongs, ...newSongs]);
          // ä¸ºæ–°å¢çš„æ­Œæ›²è·å–ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢
          newSongs.forEach((song) => {
            fetchAlbumImage(song);
          });
        }
        setTotal(data.total || 0);
        setCurrentPage(page);
        setHasMore(page * pageSize < (data.total || 0));

        // æ›´æ–°URLå‚æ•°
        if (page === 1) {
          const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
          searchParams.set("q", keyword);
          navigate(`/?${searchParams.toString()}`, { replace: true });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("æœç´¢å¤±è´¥:", error);
        message.error("æœç´¢å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åé‡è¯•");
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
        setIsLazyLoading(false);
        finishSearch(); // å®Œæˆæœç´¢åå…³é—­åŠ è½½çŠ¶æ€
      }
    },
    [searchKeyword, pageSize, location.search, navigate, finishSearch]
  );

  // é¡µé¢åŠ è½½æ—¶æ£€æŸ¥URLå‚æ•°
  useEffect(() => {
    const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
    const query = searchParams.get("q");
    if (query) {
      searchSongs(1);
    }
  }, [location.search, searchSongs]);

  // å½“æœç´¢å…³é”®è¯æ”¹å˜æ—¶è‡ªåŠ¨æœç´¢
  useEffect(() => {
    searchSongs(1);
  }, [searchSongs]); // ç§»é™¤ searchSongs ä¾èµ–ï¼Œé¿å…å‡½æ•°å˜åŒ–å¯¼è‡´é‡å¤æ‰§è¡Œ

  const loadMoreSongs = useCallback(() => {
    if (!hasMore || isLoading || isLazyLoading) return;
    setIsLazyLoading(true);
    searchSongs(currentPage + 1);
  }, [hasMore, isLoading, isLazyLoading, searchSongs, currentPage]);

  const lastSongElementRef = useCallback(
    (node) => {
      if (isLoading || isLazyLoading) return;
      if (observerRef.current) observerRef.current.disconnect();
      observerRef.current = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        if (entries[0].isIntersecting && hasMore) {
          loadMoreSongs();
        }
      });
      if (node) observerRef.current.observe(node);
    },
    [isLoading, isLazyLoading, hasMore, loadMoreSongs]
  );

  const handlePlaySong = async (song) => {
    try {
      const res = await getSongUrl(song.FileHash);
      const url = res.backupUrl[0];

      // ä½¿ç”¨æ–°çš„æ’­æ”¾å™¨ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡
      playSong(
        {
          ...song,
          title: song.OriSongName,
          artist: song.SingerName,
          album: song.AlbumName,
          url: url,
        },
        songs,
        songs.findIndex((s) => s.FileHash === song.FileHash)
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥:", error);
      message.error("æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åé‡è¯•");
    }
  };

  const handleDownload = async (song) => {
    try {
      // æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸‹è½½ä¸­æç¤º
      const downloadBtn = event.target.closest(".action-button");
      const originalText = downloadBtn.innerHTML;
      downloadBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner"></span> ä¸‹è½½ä¸­...';
      downloadBtn.disabled = true;

      // ç”Ÿæˆè§„èŒƒçš„æ–‡ä»¶å
      const filename = generateMusicFilename(song);

      // ä½¿ç”¨axiosä¸‹è½½
      const result = await downloadSong(song.FileHash, filename);

      if (result.success) {
        console.log(`ä¸‹è½½æˆåŠŸ: ${result.filename}`);
      }

      // æ¢å¤æŒ‰é’®çŠ¶æ€
      downloadBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
      downloadBtn.disabled = false;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("ä¸‹è½½å¤±è´¥:", error);
      message.error(`ä¸‹è½½å¤±è´¥: ${error.message}`);

      // æ¢å¤æŒ‰é’®çŠ¶æ€
      const downloadBtn = event.target.closest(".action-button");
      if (downloadBtn) {
        const originalText = downloadBtn.innerHTML.replace(
          '<span class="spinner"></span> ä¸‹è½½ä¸­...',
          "ğŸ“¥ ä¸‹è½½"
        );
        downloadBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
        downloadBtn.disabled = false;
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="home-container">
      {/* ç»“æœåŒºåŸŸ */}
      <div className="results-section">
        <div className="results-header">
          <h2 className="section-title">ğŸ¶ æœç´¢ç»“æœ</h2>
          {total > 0 && (
            <div className="results-info">
              <span>å…±æ‰¾åˆ° {total} é¦–æ­Œæ›²</span>
              <span>å…± {currentPage} é¡µ</span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="song-list-container">
          <Spin spinning={isLoading} size="large" tip="æœç´¢ä¸­...">
            <div className="song-list">
              {songs.length > 0 ? (
                songs.map((song, index) => (
                  <div
                    key={`${song.FileHash}-${index}`}
                    className="song-item glass-card"
                    ref={index === songs.length - 1 ? lastSongElementRef : null}
                  >
                    {/* ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢ */}
                    <div className="song-cover">
                      {albumImages[song.FileHash] ? (
                        <img
                          src={albumImages[song.FileHash]}
                          alt={song.AlbumName || "ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢"}
                          className="album-cover-img"
                          onError={(e) => {
                            e.target.style.display = "none";
                            e.target.nextSibling.style.display = "flex";
                          }}
                        />
                      ) : null}
                      <div className="album-cover-placeholder">ğŸµ</div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="song-info">
                      <div className="song-title">
                        <PlayCircleOutlined className="title-icon" />
                        {song.OriSongName}
                      </div>
                      <div className="song-meta">
                        <span className="song-artist">
                          <UserOutlined /> {song.SingerName}
                        </span>
                        <span className="song-album">
                          <DatabaseOutlined /> {song.AlbumName || "æœªçŸ¥ä¸“è¾‘"}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="song-actions">
                      <button
                        className="action-button glass-button play-btn"
                        onClick={() => handlePlaySong(song)}
                      >
                        <PlayCircleOutlined />
                        æ’­æ”¾
                      </button>
                      <button
                        className="action-button glass-button download-btn"
                        onClick={() => handleDownload(song)}
                      >
                        <DownloadOutlined />
                        ä¸‹è½½
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))
              ) : (
                <div className="no-results glass-card">
                  <Empty
                    image={Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE}
                    description={
                      searchKeyword ? "æœªæ‰¾åˆ°ç›¸å…³æ­Œæ›²" : "è¯·è¾“å…¥å…³é”®è¯å¼€å§‹æœç´¢"
                    }
                  >
                    <p
                      style={{
                        color: "rgba(255,255,255,0.7)",
                        fontSize: "0.9rem",
                      }}
                    >
                      æ”¯æŒæœç´¢æ­Œæ›²åã€æ­Œæ‰‹åã€ä¸“è¾‘å
                    </p>
                  </Empty>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </Spin>

          {/* æ‡’åŠ è½½æŒ‡ç¤ºå™¨ */}
          {isLazyLoading && (
            <div className="lazy-loading-indicator">
              <LoadingOutlined style={{ fontSize: 24, color: "#1890ff" }} />
              <span>åŠ è½½æ›´å¤šæ­Œæ›²...</span>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* æ²¡æœ‰æ›´å¤šæ•°æ®æç¤º */}
          {!hasMore && songs.length > 0 && (
            <div className="no-more-data">
              <span>æ²¡æœ‰æ›´å¤šæ­Œæ›²äº†</span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Home;

// src/hooks/useForceNavigate.js
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

export const useForceNavigate = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  
  const forceNavigate = (path, options = {}) => {
    // å¼ºåˆ¶åˆ·æ–°é¡µé¢çš„å¯¼èˆªå‡½æ•°
    const { forceRefresh = false, ...navigateOptions } = options;
    
    // å¦‚æœæ˜ç¡®è¦æ±‚å¼ºåˆ¶åˆ·æ–°ï¼Œæˆ–è€…è·¯å¾„æ˜¯ç™»å½•é¡µé¢
    if (forceRefresh || path === '/login') {
      // ç›´æ¥åˆ·æ–°æ•´ä¸ªé¡µé¢
      window.location.href = path;
    } else {
      // ä½¿ç”¨æ­£å¸¸çš„ React Router å¯¼èˆª
      navigate(path, navigateOptions);
    }
  };
  
  return forceNavigate;
};

// src/contexts/AuthContext.jsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { request } from "../services/api";
import { getToken, removeToken, setToken } from "../utils/token";

const AuthContext = createContext();

export const useAuth = () => {
  const context = useContext(AuthContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error("useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider");
  }
  return context;
};

export const AuthProvider = ({ children }) => {
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  // æ£€æŸ¥æœ¬åœ°å­˜å‚¨ä¸­çš„ç”¨æˆ·ä¿¡æ¯å¹¶éªŒè¯ token
  useEffect(() => {
    const token = getToken();
    const getUserDetail = async () => {
      // è·å–ç”¨æˆ·è¯¦ç»†ä¿¡æ¯
      try {
        const userInfo = await request(`/user/detail`);
        if (userInfo.error_code === 0 && userInfo.data) {
          setUser({
            ...token,
            profile: userInfo.data,
          });
        } else {
          // å¦‚æœè·å–è¯¦ç»†ä¿¡æ¯å¤±è´¥ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨åŸºæœ¬ä¿¡æ¯
          setUser(token);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("è·å–ç”¨æˆ·è¯¦æƒ…å¤±è´¥:", error);
        // å¤±è´¥æ—¶ä»ç„¶è®¾ç½®ç”¨æˆ·åŸºæœ¬ä¿¡æ¯
        setUser(token);
      }
    };
    const checkAuth = async () => {
      try {
        request(`/login/token?token=${token?.token}&userid=${token?.userid}`)
          .then(() => {
            console.log("Token is valid");
            getUserDetail();
          })
          .catch(() => {
            console.log("Token is invalid");
            setUser(null);
          });
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Failed to parse auth data:", error);
        localStorage.removeItem("auth");
      }
      setLoading(false);
    };

    checkAuth();
  }, []);

  const login = async (token) => {
    // å­˜å‚¨åŸºæœ¬è®¤è¯ä¿¡æ¯
    setToken(token);
  };

  const logout = () => {
    removeToken();
  };

  const value = {
    user,
    login,
    logout,
    isAuthenticated: !!user,
    loading,
  };

  return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;
};

// src/contexts/PlayerContext.jsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, useReducer, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { getAlbumImages } from '../services/api';

// åˆå§‹åŒ–éŸ³é¢‘ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ï¼ˆå¤‡ç”¨ï¼‰
// let audioContext = null;
// try {
//   audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
// } catch (e) {
//   console.warn('éŸ³é¢‘ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡åˆå§‹åŒ–å¤±è´¥:', e);
// }

// åˆå§‹çŠ¶æ€
const initialState = {
  currentSong: null,
  isPlaying: false,
  currentTime: 0,
  duration: 0,
  volume: 0.7,
  playbackRate: 1.0,
  playlist: [],
  currentIndex: -1,
  isLoading: false,
  error: null
};

// æ’­æ”¾å™¨åŠ¨ä½œç±»å‹
const ACTIONS = {
  SET_CURRENT_SONG: 'SET_CURRENT_SONG',
  TOGGLE_PLAY: 'TOGGLE_PLAY',
  PLAY: 'PLAY',
  PAUSE: 'PAUSE',
  SET_TIME: 'SET_TIME',
  SET_DURATION: 'SET_DURATION',
  SET_VOLUME: 'SET_VOLUME',
  SET_PLAYBACK_RATE: 'SET_PLAYBACK_RATE',
  SET_PLAYLIST: 'SET_PLAYLIST',
  SET_CURRENT_INDEX: 'SET_CURRENT_INDEX',
  SET_LOADING: 'SET_LOADING',
  SET_ERROR: 'SET_ERROR',
  NEXT_SONG: 'NEXT_SONG',
  PREV_SONG: 'PREV_SONG'
};

// Reducer å‡½æ•°
const playerReducer = (state, action) => {
  switch (action.type) {
    case ACTIONS.SET_CURRENT_SONG:
      return {
        ...state,
        currentSong: action.payload,
        currentTime: 0,
        error: null
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.TOGGLE_PLAY:
      return {
        ...state,
        isPlaying: !state.isPlaying
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.PLAY:
      return {
        ...state,
        isPlaying: true
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.PAUSE:
      return {
        ...state,
        isPlaying: false
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_TIME:
      return {
        ...state,
        currentTime: action.payload
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_DURATION:
      return {
        ...state,
        duration: action.payload
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_VOLUME:
      return {
        ...state,
        volume: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, action.payload))
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_PLAYBACK_RATE:
      return {
        ...state,
        playbackRate: action.payload
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_PLAYLIST:
      return {
        ...state,
        playlist: action.payload,
        currentIndex: action.payload.length > 0 ? 0 : -1
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_CURRENT_INDEX:
      return {
        ...state,
        currentIndex: action.payload,
        currentSong: action.payload >= 0 && action.payload < state.playlist.length 
          ? state.playlist[action.payload] 
          : null,
        currentTime: 0
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_LOADING:
      return {
        ...state,
        isLoading: action.payload
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.SET_ERROR:
      return {
        ...state,
        error: action.payload,
        isLoading: false
      };
    
    case ACTIONS.NEXT_SONG: {
      const nextIndex = state.currentIndex + 1;
      if (nextIndex < state.playlist.length) {
        return {
          ...state,
          currentIndex: nextIndex,
          currentSong: state.playlist[nextIndex],
          currentTime: 0,
          isPlaying: true
        };
      }
      return state;
    }
    
    case ACTIONS.PREV_SONG: {
      const prevIndex = state.currentIndex - 1;
      if (prevIndex >= 0) {
        return {
          ...state,
          currentIndex: prevIndex,
          currentSong: state.playlist[prevIndex],
          currentTime: 0,
          isPlaying: true
        };
      }
      return state;
    }
    
    default:
      return state;
  }
};

// åˆ›å»º Context
const PlayerContext = createContext();

// Provider ç»„ä»¶
export const PlayerProvider = ({ children }) => {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(playerReducer, initialState);
  const audioRef = useRef(null);

  // è·å–ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢
  const fetchAlbumCover = async (song) => {
    try {
      const res = await getAlbumImages(song.FileHash, song.AlbumID || '');
      console.log('åº•éƒ¨æ’­æ”¾æ ä¸“è¾‘å›¾ç‰‡APIå“åº”:', res);
      
      if (res.data && res.data.length > 0) {
        let imageUrl = '';
        
        // ä¼˜å…ˆæ£€æŸ¥ album æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„ sizable_cover
        if (res.data[0].album && res.data[0].album.length > 0) {
          const album = res.data[0].album[0];
          imageUrl = album.sizable_cover || '';
          if (imageUrl) {
            imageUrl = imageUrl.replace('{size}', '200');
          }
        }
        
        // å¦‚æœ album ä¸­æ²¡æœ‰æ‰¾åˆ°ï¼Œæ£€æŸ¥ author ä¸­çš„å›¾ç‰‡
        if (!imageUrl && res.data[0].author && res.data[0].author.length > 0) {
          const author = res.data[0].author[0];
          
          // ä¼˜å…ˆä½¿ç”¨ imgs['3'] ä¸­çš„å›¾ç‰‡
          if (author.imgs && author.imgs['3'] && author.imgs['3'].length > 0) {
            imageUrl = author.imgs['3'][0]?.sizable_portrait || '';
            if (imageUrl) {
              imageUrl = imageUrl.replace('{size}', '200');
            }
          } 
          // å…¶æ¬¡ä½¿ç”¨ imgs['4'] ä¸­çš„å›¾ç‰‡
          else if (author.imgs && author.imgs['4'] && author.imgs['4'].length > 0) {
            imageUrl = author.imgs['4'][0]?.sizable_portrait || '';
            if (imageUrl) {
              imageUrl = imageUrl.replace('{size}', '200');
            }
          }
          // æœ€åä½¿ç”¨ avatar
          else if (author.sizable_avatar) {
            imageUrl = author.sizable_avatar.replace('{size}', '200');
          }
        }
        
        if (imageUrl) {
          console.log(`ä¸ºæ’­æ”¾æ­Œæ›² ${song.OriSongName} è®¾ç½®å°é¢:`, imageUrl);
          return imageUrl;
        }
      }
      return null;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('è·å–æ’­æ”¾æ­Œæ›²ä¸“è¾‘å›¾ç‰‡å¤±è´¥:', error);
      return null;
    }
  };

  // æ’­æ”¾å™¨æ“ä½œå‡½æ•°
  const playSong = async (song, playlist = [], index = 0) => {
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_LOADING, payload: true });
    
    if (playlist.length > 0) {
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_PLAYLIST, payload: playlist });
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_CURRENT_INDEX, payload: index });
    }
    
    // è·å–ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢
    const albumCover = await fetchAlbumCover(song);
    
    // å°†ä¸“è¾‘å°é¢æ·»åŠ åˆ°æ­Œæ›²å¯¹è±¡ä¸­
    const songWithCover = {
      ...song,
      thumbnail: albumCover || song.thumbnail
    };
    
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_CURRENT_SONG, payload: songWithCover });
    
    // è®¾ç½®éŸ³é¢‘æº
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.src = song.url || song.preview_url;
      audioRef.current.load();
      
      // ç›‘å¬åŠ è½½å®Œæˆäº‹ä»¶
      const handleLoadedMetadata = () => {
        dispatch({ 
          type: ACTIONS.SET_DURATION, 
          payload: audioRef.current.duration || 0 
        });
        dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_LOADING, payload: false });
        
        // è‡ªåŠ¨æ’­æ”¾
        audioRef.current.play()
          .then(() => {
            dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PLAY });
          })
          .catch(error => {
            console.error('æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥:', error);
            dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_ERROR, payload: 'æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥' });
            dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_LOADING, payload: false });
          });
      };
      
      const handleError = (e) => {
        console.error('éŸ³é¢‘åŠ è½½é”™è¯¯:', e);
        dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_ERROR, payload: 'éŸ³é¢‘åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥' });
        dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_LOADING, payload: false });
      };
      
      audioRef.current.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', handleLoadedMetadata, { once: true });
      audioRef.current.addEventListener('error', handleError, { once: true });
    }
  };

  const togglePlay = () => {
    if (!state.currentSong) return;
    
    if (state.isPlaying) {
      audioRef.current?.pause();
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PAUSE });
    } else {
      audioRef.current?.play()
        .then(() => {
          dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PLAY });
        })
        .catch(error => {
          console.error('æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥:', error);
          dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_ERROR, payload: 'æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥' });
        });
    }
  };

  const pause = () => {
    audioRef.current?.pause();
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PAUSE });
  };

  const play = () => {
    if (state.currentSong) {
      audioRef.current?.play()
        .then(() => {
          dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PLAY });
        })
        .catch(error => {
          console.error('æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥:', error);
          dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_ERROR, payload: 'æ’­æ”¾å¤±è´¥' });
        });
    }
  };

  const seekTo = (time) => {
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.currentTime = time;
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_TIME, payload: time });
    }
  };

  const setVolume = (volume) => {
    const vol = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, volume));
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.volume = vol;
    }
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_VOLUME, payload: vol });
  };

  const setPlaybackRate = (rate) => {
    const validRate = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2, rate));
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.playbackRate = validRate;
    }
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_PLAYBACK_RATE, payload: validRate });
  };

  const nextSong = () => {
    if (state.currentIndex < state.playlist.length - 1) {
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.NEXT_SONG });
    }
  };

  const prevSong = () => {
    if (state.currentIndex > 0) {
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PREV_SONG });
    }
  };

  const setCurrentTime = (time) => {
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_TIME, payload: time });
  };

  const addToPlaylist = (songs) => {
    const newPlaylist = [...state.playlist, ...songs];
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_PLAYLIST, payload: newPlaylist });
  };

  const clearPlaylist = () => {
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_PLAYLIST, payload: [] });
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_CURRENT_SONG, payload: null });
    dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PAUSE });
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.src = '';
    }
  };

  // éŸ³é¢‘äº‹ä»¶å¤„ç†
  useEffect(() => {
    const audio = audioRef.current;
    if (!audio) return;

    const handleTimeUpdate = () => {
      setCurrentTime(audio.currentTime);
    };

    const handleEnded = () => {
      // æ­Œæ›²ç»“æŸæ—¶è‡ªåŠ¨æ’­æ”¾ä¸‹ä¸€é¦–æˆ–æš‚åœ
      if (state.currentIndex < state.playlist.length - 1) {
        dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.NEXT_SONG });
      } else {
        dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PAUSE });
        // æ’­æ”¾å®Œæ¯•åæ¸…é™¤å½“å‰æ­Œæ›²ï¼Œéšè—æ’­æ”¾å™¨
        setTimeout(() => {
          dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_CURRENT_SONG, payload: null });
        }, 1000); // å»¶è¿Ÿ1ç§’åå…³é—­æ’­æ”¾æ ï¼Œè®©ç”¨æˆ·çœ‹åˆ°æ’­æ”¾å®Œæˆçš„çŠ¶æ€
      }
    };

    const handleError = (e) => {
      console.error('éŸ³é¢‘æ’­æ”¾é”™è¯¯:', e);
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.SET_ERROR, payload: 'æ’­æ”¾å‡ºé”™' });
      dispatch({ type: ACTIONS.PAUSE });
    };

    audio.addEventListener('timeupdate', handleTimeUpdate);
    audio.addEventListener('ended', handleEnded);
    audio.addEventListener('error', handleError);

    // æ¸…ç†äº‹ä»¶ç›‘å¬å™¨
    return () => {
      audio.removeEventListener('timeupdate', handleTimeUpdate);
      audio.removeEventListener('ended', handleEnded);
      audio.removeEventListener('error', handleError);
    };
  }, [state.currentIndex, state.playlist.length, dispatch, setCurrentTime]);

  // åŒæ­¥éŸ³é‡è®¾ç½®
  useEffect(() => {
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.volume = state.volume;
    }
  }, [state.volume]);

  // åŒæ­¥æ’­æ”¾é€Ÿç‡è®¾ç½®
  useEffect(() => {
    if (audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.playbackRate = state.playbackRate;
    }
  }, [state.playbackRate]);

  // Context å€¼
  const value = {
    // çŠ¶æ€
    ...state,
    // å¼•ç”¨
    audioRef,
    // æ“ä½œå‡½æ•°
    playSong,
    togglePlay,
    play,
    pause,
    seekTo,
    setVolume,
    setPlaybackRate,
    nextSong,
    prevSong,
    setCurrentTime,
    addToPlaylist,
    clearPlaylist
  };

  return (
    <PlayerContext.Provider value={value}>
      {children}
      {/* éšè—çš„éŸ³é¢‘å…ƒç´  */}
      <audio ref={audioRef} preload="metadata" />
    </PlayerContext.Provider>
  );
};

// è‡ªå®šä¹‰ Hook
export const usePlayer = () => {
  const context = useContext(PlayerContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('usePlayer å¿…é¡»åœ¨ PlayerProvider å†…éƒ¨ä½¿ç”¨');
  }
  return context;
};

export default PlayerContext;

// src/contexts/SearchContext.jsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { message } from "antd";

const SearchContext = createContext();

export const useSearch = () => {
  const context = useContext(SearchContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error("useSearch must be used within a SearchProvider");
  }
  return context;
};

export const SearchProvider = ({ children }) => {
  const [searchKeyword, setSearchKeyword] = useState("");
  const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);

  const handleSearch = useCallback((keyword) => {
    if (!keyword?.trim()) {
      message.warning("è¯·è¾“å…¥æœç´¢å…³é”®è¯");
      return;
    }
    if (keyword !== searchKeyword) {
      setSearchKeyword(keyword.trim());
      setIsSearching(true);
    }

    // æœç´¢çŠ¶æ€ç”±ä½¿ç”¨æœç´¢ç»“æœçš„ç»„ä»¶æ¥æ§åˆ¶
  }, [searchKeyword]);

  const clearSearch = useCallback(() => {
    setSearchKeyword("");
    setIsSearching(false);
  }, []);

  const finishSearch = useCallback(() => {
    setIsSearching(false);
  }, []);

  const value = {
    searchKeyword,
    isSearching,
    handleSearch,
    clearSearch,
    finishSearch,
    setSearchKeyword,
  };

  return (
    <SearchContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</SearchContext.Provider>
  );
};

// src/components/AppLayout.jsx
import React from 'react';

import { useForceNavigate } from '../hooks/useForceNavigate';

const AppLayout = ({ children }) => {
  const { isAuthenticated, loading } = useAuth();
  const forceNavigate = useForceNavigate();
  
  if (loading) {
    return <div className="loading">åŠ è½½ä¸­...</div>;
  }
  
  if (!isAuthenticated) {
    // å¦‚æœæœªè®¤è¯ï¼Œå¼ºåˆ¶åˆ·æ–°é‡å®šå‘åˆ°ç™»å½•é¡µé¢
    forceNavigate('/login', { forceRefresh: true });
    return null; // è¿”å› null å› ä¸ºé¡µé¢å³å°†åˆ·æ–°
  }
  
  return (
    <Layout>
      {children || <Outlet />}
    </Layout>
  );
};

export default AppLayout;

// src/components/BottomPlayer.jsx
import React from 'react';

import { usePlayer } from '../contexts/PlayerContext';

const BottomPlayer = () => {
  const {
    currentSong,
    isPlaying,
    currentTime,
    duration,
    volume,
    isLoading,
    error,
    togglePlay,
    // pause,
    // play,
    seekTo,
    setVolume
    // nextSong,
    // prevSong
  } = usePlayer();

  // è®¡ç®—è¿›åº¦ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”
  const progressPercent = duration > 0 ? (currentTime / duration) * 100 : 0;

  // æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ—¶é—´æ˜¾ç¤º
  const formatTime = (seconds) => {
    if (isNaN(seconds) || seconds === Infinity) return '0:00';
    const mins = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
    const secs = Math.floor(seconds % 60);
    return `${mins}:${secs.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
  };

  // å¤„ç†è¿›åº¦æ¡ç‚¹å‡»
  const handleProgressClick = (e) => {
    if (!currentSong || duration <= 0) return;
    
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    const clickX = e.clientX - rect.left;
    const percentage = clickX / rect.width;
    const newTime = percentage * duration;
    
    seekTo(newTime);
  };

  // å¤„ç†éŸ³é‡æ»‘å—å˜åŒ–
  const handleVolumeChange = (e) => {
    const newVolume = parseFloat(e.target.value);
    setVolume(newVolume);
  };

  // å¤„ç†éŸ³é‡å›¾æ ‡ç‚¹å‡»
  const toggleMute = () => {
    if (volume > 0) {
      setVolume(0);
    } else {
      setVolume(0.7);
    }
  };

  // å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰å½“å‰æ­Œæ›²ï¼Œåˆ™ä¸æ˜¾ç¤ºæ’­æ”¾å™¨
  if (!currentSong) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div className="bottom-player">
      {/* è¿›åº¦æ¡ */}
      <div className="player-progress-bar" onClick={handleProgressClick}>
        <div 
          className="progress-fill" 
          style={{ width: `${progressPercent}%` }}
        ></div>
      </div>

      <div className="player-container glass-effect">
        <div className="player-content">
          {/* æ­Œæ›²ä¿¡æ¯ */}
          <div className="song-info">
            <div className="song-cover">
              {currentSong.thumbnail ? (
                <img 
                  src={currentSong.thumbnail} 
                  alt={currentSong.title}
                  className="album-cover-img"
                  onError={(e) => {
                    e.target.style.display = 'none';
                    e.target.nextSibling.style.display = 'flex';
                  }}
                />
              ) : null}
              <div className="album-cover-placeholder">
                ğŸµ
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="song-details">
              <div className="song-title" title={currentSong.title}>
                {currentSong.title || 'æœªçŸ¥æ­Œæ›²'}
              </div>
              <div className="song-artist" title={currentSong.artist}>
                {currentSong.artist || 'æœªçŸ¥è‰ºæœ¯å®¶'}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* æ§åˆ¶æŒ‰é’® */}
          <div className="player-controls">

            
            <button 
              className="control-btn play-btn glass-button"
              onClick={togglePlay}
              disabled={isLoading}
              title={isPlaying ? 'æš‚åœ' : 'æ’­æ”¾'}
            >
              {isLoading ? (
                <div className="loading-spinner"></div>
              ) : isPlaying ? (
                <span className="play-icon play-pause-icon">â¸</span>
              ) : (
                <span className="play-icon play-pause-icon">â–¶</span>
              )}
            </button>

          </div>

          {/* æ—¶é—´æ˜¾ç¤ºå’ŒéŸ³é‡æ§åˆ¶ */}
          <div className="player-extras">
            <div className="time-display">
              <span>{formatTime(currentTime)}</span>
              <span>/</span>
              <span>{formatTime(duration)}</span>
            </div>
            
            <div className="volume-control">
              <button 
                className="volume-btn glass-button"
                onClick={toggleMute}
                title={volume > 0 ? 'é™éŸ³' : 'å–æ¶ˆé™éŸ³'}
              >
                {volume > 0 ? 'ğŸ”Š' : 'ğŸ”‡'}
              </button>
              
              <div className="volume-slider-container">
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="0"
                  max="1"
                  step="0.01"
                  value={volume}
                  onChange={handleVolumeChange}
                  className="volume-slider"
                />
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* é”™è¯¯æç¤º */}
        {error && (
          <div className="player-error">
            âš ï¸ {error}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default BottomPlayer;

              to="/"

            >
              é¦–é¡µ
            </Link>

                <div className="user-profile">

// src/components/Login.jsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { message } from 'antd';
import { useAuth } from '../contexts/AuthContext';
import { request } from '../services/api';

export default function Login() {
  
  const [mobile, setMobile] = useState('');
  const [code, setCode] = useState('');
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [countdown, setCountdown] = useState(0);
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { isAuthenticated, login } = useAuth();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isAuthenticated) {
      navigate('/', { replace: true });
    }
  }, [isAuthenticated, navigate]);

  useEffect(() => {
    let timer;
    if (countdown > 0) {
      timer = setTimeout(() => setCountdown(countdown - 1), 1000);
    }
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [countdown]);

  const handleSendCode = async () => {
    if (!mobile) {
      message.warning('è¯·è¾“å…¥æ‰‹æœºå·');
      return;
    }
    
    if (countdown > 0) return;
    
    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      await request(`/captcha/sent?mobile=${mobile}`);
      setCountdown(60);
      message.success('éªŒè¯ç å·²å‘é€');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('å‘é€éªŒè¯ç å¤±è´¥:', error);
      message.error('å‘é€å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åé‡è¯•');
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const handleLogin = async () => {
    if (!mobile || !code) {
      message.warning('è¯·è¾“å…¥æ‰‹æœºå·å’ŒéªŒè¯ç ');
      return;
    }

    try {
      setIsLoading(true);
      const res = await request(`/login/cellphone?mobile=${mobile}&code=${code}`);
      const data = res.data;
      login(data);
      navigate('/', { replace: true });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('ç™»å½•å¤±è´¥:', error);
      message.error('ç™»å½•å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·æ£€æŸ¥æ‰‹æœºå·å’ŒéªŒè¯ç ');
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="login-container">
      <div className="login-background">
        <div className="gradient-overlay"></div>
        <div className="floating-elements">
          {[...Array(5)].map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className={`floating-element element-${i + 1}`}></div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="login-card glass-effect">
        <div className="login-header">
          <h1 className="login-title">éŸ³ä¹ä¸‹è½½å™¨</h1>
          <p className="login-subtitle">ç•…äº«é«˜å“è´¨éŸ³ä¹ä½“éªŒ</p>
        </div>
        
        <div className="login-form">
          <div className="input-group">
            <label htmlFor="mobile">æ‰‹æœºå·</label>
            <div className="input-wrapper">
              <span className="input-icon">ğŸ“±</span>
              <input 
                id="mobile"
                type="tel" 
                placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥æ‰‹æœºå·" 
                value={mobile} 
                onChange={e => setMobile(e.target.value)}
                className="glass-input"
                disabled={isLoading}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="input-group">
            <label htmlFor="code">éªŒè¯ç </label>
            <div className="input-wrapper code-wrapper">
              <span className="input-icon">ğŸ”’</span>
              <input 
                id="code"
                type="text" 
                placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥éªŒè¯ç " 
                value={code} 
                onChange={e => setCode(e.target.value)}
                className="glass-input"
                disabled={isLoading}
              />
              <button 
                onClick={handleSendCode}
                disabled={isLoading || countdown > 0}
                className="send-code-btn glass-button primary"
              >
                {countdown > 0 ? `${countdown}s` : 'è·å–éªŒè¯ç '}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <button 
            onClick={handleLogin}
            disabled={isLoading}
            className="login-button glass-button primary"
          >
            {isLoading ? (
              <>
                <span className="spinner"></span>
                ç™»å½•ä¸­...
              </>
            ) : 'ç«‹å³ç™»å½•'}
          </button>
        </div>
        
        <div className="login-footer">
          <p>ç™»å½•å³è¡¨ç¤ºæ‚¨åŒæ„æˆ‘ä»¬çš„æœåŠ¡æ¡æ¬¾</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
